# A "compare-free" experiment

Following the success of `feedforward-run-3`.

The resulting sparsified models
  * reminded us that one can craft a hand-made solution without `compare` neuron
  * used `compare` neurons in rather strange and interesting ways (something to investigate further)

Therefore, let's try to exclude `compare` neurons from the `trainable` network signature
altogether and see what would happen.

Let's add an extra layer to make the task of finding a small model a bit more difficult (now, that there is no option
to recruit `compare` neurons as strange kinds of multipliers).

```
julia> cd("Desktop/GitHub/sandbox_mishka/arxiv-1606-09470-section3/v0-1/compare-free")
```
